      "cell_type": "code",
      "source": [
        "# Import libraries\n",
        "import pandas as pd\n",
        "import pickle\n",
        "from IPython.display import display\n",
        "\n",
        "# Load movies dataset (make sure you uploaded movies.csv in Colab)\n",
        "movies = pd.read_csv('movies.csv')\n",
        "\n",
        "# Load similarity matrix (make sure similarity.pkl is uploaded)\n",
        "with open('similarity.pkl', 'rb') as f:\n",
        "    similarity = pickle.load(f)\n",
        "\n",
        "# Helper: extract all unique genres\n",
        "all_genres = set()\n",
        "for genre_list in movies['genres']:\n",
        "    if isinstance(genre_list, str):\n",
        "        for genre in genre_list.split('|'):\n",
        "            all_genres.add(genre)\n",
        "all_genres = sorted(all_genres)\n",
        "\n",
        "print(f\"Available genres: {all_genres}\")\n",
        "\n",
        "# Function to recommend movies by movie title and genre filter\n",
        "def recommend(movie_title, selected_genre='All', top_n=10):\n",
        "    # Find the movie index in the dataset\n",
        "    movie_idx = movies[movies['title'].str.lower() == movie_title.lower()].index\n",
        "\n",
        "    if len(movie_idx) == 0:\n",
        "        print(\"Movie not found!\")\n",
        "        return []\n",
        "    movie_idx = movie_idx[0]\n",
        "\n",
        "    # Filter movies by genre if selected_genre is not 'All'\n",
        "    if selected_genre != 'All':\n",
        "        filtered_movies = movies[movies['genres'].str.contains(selected_genre, na=False)].copy()\n",
        "        filtered_indices = filtered_movies.index.tolist()\n",
        "\n",
        "        # Filter similarity matrix to only movies in selected genre\n",
        "        filtered_similarity = similarity[filtered_indices, :][:, filtered_indices]\n",
        "\n",
        "        # Adjust movie index to filtered matrix index\n",
        "        if movie_idx not in filtered_indices:\n",
        "            print(f\"Selected movie is not in genre '{selected_genre}'. Try another movie or genre.\")\n",
        "            return []\n",
        "        filtered_movie_idx = filtered_indices.index(movie_idx)\n",
        "\n",
        "        # Get similarity scores from filtered matrix\n",
        "        sim_scores = list(enumerate(filtered_similarity[filtered_movie_idx]))\n",
        "\n",
        "        # Sort by similarity score descending, ignore the movie itself\n",
        "        sim_scores = sorted(sim_scores, key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)\n",
        "        sim_scores = [s for s in sim_scores if s[0] != filtered_movie_idx]\n",
        "\n",
        "        # Top N similar movies in filtered list\n",
        "        top_similar = sim_scores[:top_n]\n",
        "\n",
        "        # Map back to original movie indices\n",
        "        recommended_indices = [filtered_indices[i[0]] for i in top_similar]\n",
        "\n",
        "    else:\n",
        "        # No genre filter: use full similarity matrix\n",
        "        sim_scores = list(enumerate(similarity[movie_idx]))\n",
        "        sim_scores = sorted(sim_scores, key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)\n",
        "        sim_scores = [s for s in sim_scores if s[0] != movie_idx]\n",
        "        recommended_indices = [i[0] for i in sim_scores[:top_n]]\n",
        "\n",
        "    # Return movie titles and genres\n",
        "    recommendations = []\n",
        "    for idx in recommended_indices:\n",
        "        title = movies.loc[idx, 'title']\n",
        "        genres = movies.loc[idx, 'genres']\n",
        "        recommendations.append((title, genres))\n",
        "\n",
        "    return recommendations\n",
        "\n",
        "\n",
        "# Example usage\n",
        "\n",
        "print(\"\\nAvailable genres:\", ['All'] + all_genres)\n",
        "print(\"Enter movie title and genre to get recommendations.\\n\")\n",
        "\n",
        "# You can change these inputs:\n",
        "movie_name = 'Toy Story (1995)'  # example movie\n",
        "genre_filter = 'Animation'       # example genre, or 'All'\n",
        "\n",
        "print(f\"Recommendations for '{movie_name}' in genre '{genre_filter}':\\n\")\n",
        "\n",
        "recs = recommend(movie_name, selected_genre=genre_filter, top_n=10)\n",
        "\n",
        "for i, (title, genres) in enumerate(recs, 1):\n",
        "    print(f\"{i}. {title} ({genres})\")\n"
      ],
